### [1] [RAMS: Resource-Adaptive and Detection-Conditioned Model Switching for Embedded Edge Perception](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14716)
*Kushal Khemani,Evan Leri,George Xu,Amit Hod*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出RAMS运行时控制器，在嵌入设备上根据资源压力与检测事件动态切换三档YOLOv8模型，无需重载，兼顾延迟与安全相关(VRU)精度；并给出无需标注的SWAS指标与其oracle变体，用于策略对比。实验证明在多平台广泛适用，尤其在Jetson Orin重载下以安全策略显著降延迟并较好保持代理精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 边缘设备资源波动大，固定模型大小难以同时满足低延迟与交通安全场景中对易受伤道路使用者(VRU)的检测需求；现有自适应方案常需重载模型或缺乏对安全事件的优先保障与可比评估指标。

Method: 设计RAMS轻量控制器：监测设备压力，基于空闲期校准阈值，常驻三档YOLOv8 (N/S/M，输入分辨率320/416/640) 并动态无重载切换；定义五种切换策略，其中两种“检测条件化”策略在近期检测到VRU时抑制降档；提出SWAS(含oracle上界)指标，用检测输出来加权评估策略在无标注下的准确性保持。跨Raspberry Pi 5、x86、Jetson Orin的ONNX/TensorRT实现，统一控制方程运行。

Result: 在Jetson Orin TensorRT重载场景下，“safety2”策略均延3.41 ms，比固定MEDIUM推理快5.6倍；在主要运行近NANO档位并在VRU阳性窗口短时锁定SMALL/MEDIUM时，保留MEDIUM代理精度的74%。检测条件化切换在重载下相较仅阈值策略，SWAS提高25.4%(oracle)与47.3%(检测派生)。KITTI在线评估显示各档VRU召回为24.2%/41.2%/59.0%，揭示反应式覆盖受基线召回的根本限制。

Conclusion: RAMS在大幅降低延迟的同时，通过事件感知的策略维持对VRU的相对精度，且跨硬件通用；SWAS及其oracle变体为无标注离线对比提供依据。但整体安全性仍受底层检测器召回限制，提示需提升基础模型或引入前瞻性机制以突破上限。

Abstract: Edge object detection on embedded hardware requires balancing inference latency and detection quality under changing resource pressure. We present RAMS, a lightweight runtime controller that monitors device pressure, calibrates switching thresholds from idle behavior, and dynamically selects among three resident YOLOv8 tiers (NANO/SMALL/MEDIUM at 320/416/640 px) without model-reload latency. RAMS defines five switching policies, including two detection-conditioned variants that prevent aggressive downgrades after recent vulnerable-road-user (VRU) detections. We further introduce the VRU-Weighted Accuracy Score (SWAS), a scalar metric for offline policy comparison without ground-truth annotations, together with an oracle-bounded variant that separates detector circularity from genuine tier-retention benefit. Across Raspberry Pi 5, x86 laptops, and Jetson Orin ONNX/TensorRT deployments, the same controller equations operate over a 37x latency range. On Jetson Orin TensorRT under heavy load, the safety2 policy achieves 3.41 ms mean latency, 5.6x faster than fixed-MEDIUM inference, while retaining 74% of its proxy accuracy through near-NANO operation with selective SMALL and MEDIUM locks during VRU-positive windows. Detection-conditioned switching improves SWAS by 25.4% under oracle scoring and 47.3% under detector-derived scoring relative to threshold-only policies under heavy load. Live KITTI evaluation reports per-tier VRU recall of 24.2%, 41.2%, and 59.0%, showing that reactive overrides are fundamentally limited by baseline detector recall.

</details>


### [2] [AI for Maritime Security: Comparative Evaluation of CNN and Vision Transformer Architectures for Maritime Object Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14720)
*Ismet Gocer,Zakirul Bhuiayn,Shakeel Ahmad,Raza Hasan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 评估六种深度学习与Transformer架构在多天气海面船只检测任务上的表现，ViT在准确率、错误率与视频处理速度上综合最优，轻量模型适用于算力受限场景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 提升海上安全与监视能力，需要在多变天气和实时环境下可靠检测海面船只；现有方法在复杂条件与部署资源受限情况下性能与效率权衡不足。

Method: 构建含6,468张、覆盖多种天气（多云、雾、雨、晴）的海事图像数据集；评估六种模型：自建CNN、四个迁移学习模型（Xception、VGG16、MobileNetV2、EfficientNetV2L）与Vision Transformer（ViT）；以准确率、I类/II类错误、模型大小与视频处理时间为指标比较。

Result: 不同模型在算力与部署条件下表现差异明显；轻量架构更适合资源受限设备；ViT取得综合最佳：报告称达100%准确率、最低错误率，并具备最快视频处理速度。

Conclusion: AI驱动的计算机视觉方案可显著增强海上监视、边境保护与自主航行能力；在实际部署需依据算力与场景选择模型，但ViT在该数据集上显示出最优潜力。

Abstract: This study aims to enhance maritime security by using advanced Artificial Intelligence (AI) and Computer Vision (CV) techniques. For this purpose, it was designed and assessed intelligent object detection systems that can detect the presence of ships on the sea surface under different real-time environments. To achieve this goal, a maritime image dataset with 6,468 images was used, covering different weather conditions like cloudy, foggy, rainy, and sunny environments. Six deep learning architectures were evaluated, including a base Convolutional Neural Network (CNN) model, four transfer learning models (Xception, VGG16, MobileNetV2, and EfficientNetV2L), and a Vision Transformer (ViT) model. The models were compared using multiple performance indicators, including accuracy, Type I and Type II errors, model size, and video processing time. The results show that model performance varies depending on computational constraints and deployment conditions. While lightweight architectures are suitable for resource-limited devices, the ViT achieved the best overall performance, reaching 100% accuracy with the lowest error rates and the fastest video processing time. The findings highlight the potential of AI-driven computer vision systems for maritime surveillance, border protection, and autonomous navigation.

</details>


### [3] [Disagreement-Based Cross-Model Routing for Implicit Video Question Answering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14723)
*Durga Sandeep Saluru*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文提出在ImplicitQA视频多选问答上，用“分歧驱动的跨模型路由”替代常规自洽多数投票：先对主视频模型做三次零温采样，凡三次答案不一致的问题（约20%）再转交给另一家族的模型作答。无需训练与标注，仅推理时策略，即可在验证集提升平均准确率约+1.43；在更依赖跨镜头参照的问题类别（运动轨迹、推断计数、垂直空间）提升更显著，并在独立挑战测试集复现增益（82.03 AvgAcc / 79.71 MacroAvgAcc，较最佳单样本+1.81）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ImplicitQA答案不直接出现在画面中，需要基于镜外事件、视线、因果与跨镜头空间关系进行推断。前沿视频LLM在该基准上已接近上限，常规自洽（多次采样多数投票）因难题上的相关性错误会恶化结果。需要一种不依赖训练与标注、能在推理时有针对性纠错的策略。

Method: 1) 使用主视频模型（Gemini 3.1 Pro Preview）在温度0下三次独立采样，利用其视频处理流水线带来的自然样本差异。2) 识别答案出现分歧的约20%问题。3) 仅将这部分问题路由给第二模型（Claude Opus 4.8），该模型基于均匀采样帧并采用自适应思考进行回答。4) 其余80%保留主模型单样本答案。全流程纯推理时，无需额外训练或标签。

Result: 在含1001题且有公开标注的验证集上，平均准确率较主模型最佳单样本提升+1.43；类别增益集中于运动与轨迹(+5.49)、推断计数(+3.45)、垂直空间推理(+1.82)。在独立的172题CVPR 2026挑战测试集上，取得82.03 AvgAcc / 79.71 MacroAvgAcc，较主模型最佳单样本+1.81。

Conclusion: 通过“分歧识别+跨模型路由”，可在无需训练与标注的前提下突破单模型与多数投票的瓶颈，尤其改善依赖跨镜头参照解析的隐式推理题型，验证与独立测试集均证明其稳健有效。

Abstract: We study multiple-choice video question answering on the ImplicitQA benchmark, where the correct answer is never explicitly shown but must be inferred from off-screen events, line-of-sight cues, causal structure, and cross-shot spatial layout. On this benchmark a single frontier video LLM already operates near its accuracy ceiling, and we observe that conventional self-consistency strategies -- majority voting across repeated samples of the same model -- can hurt rather than help, because the model's errors on hard questions are correlated. We propose disagreement-based cross-model routing, a pure inference-time procedure that requires no labels and no training. We triple-sample a native-video model (Gemini 3.1 Pro Preview) at temperature zero, exploit the genuine sample-to-sample variance of its video-processing pipeline to identify the roughly 20% subset of questions where the three samples disagree, and route only that subset to a second model from a different family (Claude Opus 4.8) that consumes uniformly sampled frames with adaptive thinking. On the 1001-question validation set with public ground truth -- our main evaluation -- the method improves AvgAcc by +1.43 over the best single sample of the primary model, with per-category gains concentrated on Motion & Trajectory (+5.49), Inferred Counting (+3.45), and Vertical Spatial Reasoning (+1.82) -- the categories most dependent on cross-shot reference resolution. The same pipeline applied to the held-out 172-question CVPR 2026 ImplicitQA challenge test set achieves 82.03 AvgAcc / 79.71 MacroAvgAcc (+1.81 over the best single sample of the primary model), confirming the validation result on an independent split.

</details>


### [4] [VigilFormer: Deformable Attention for Video Anomaly Detection with Causal Risk Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14724)
*Xinze Zhang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: VigilFormer提出结合可变形时空注意力与因果时间建模，用弱监督在监控视频中高效检测异常，并通过自适应跳帧在推理时提升速度，在多个数据集上实现更高AUC与41.5 FPS的实时性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有监控视频异常检测要在精度与实时性间权衡：强特征提取器提升精度但代价高，轻量结构高效但易丢失复杂时空模式。作者希望在弱监督条件下同时兼顾准确性与吞吐。

Method: 1) 可变形时空编码器DSTE：跨帧对少量关键位置执行稀疏注意力，保留不规则运动建模能力并避免密集注意力的二次复杂度；2) 因果异常分类器CAC：对片段级特征用膨胀因果卷积，配合对比式多示例学习目标，在无帧级标注下区分异常与正常表示；3) 自适应置信度调度ACS：推理时动态跳过低信息帧，降低静态场景的冗余计算。

Result: 在UCF-Crime、ShanghaiTech、CUHK Avenue上分别达到AUC 87.83%、97.21%、89.74%，单卡41.5 FPS，较近期弱监督方法在准确度与速度上均有优势。

Conclusion: 结合可变形时空注意与因果建模、并在推理端进行自适应跳帧，可在弱监督下实现对未剪辑监控视频的高精度与实时异常检测。

Abstract: Video anomaly detection in surveillance settings must balance detection accuracy against real-time throughput, a tension that existing methods address either through stronger feature extractors or more efficient architectures, but rarely both. We present VigilFormer, a unified framework that combines deformable spatio-temporal attention with causal temporal modeling to detect anomalies in untrimmed surveillance video. The proposed Deformable Spatio-Temporal Encoder (DSTE) attends to a sparse set of informative locations across frames, avoiding the quadratic cost of dense attention while retaining the ability to capture irregular motion patterns. A Causal Anomaly Classifier (CAC) applies dilated causal convolutions over snippet-level features and optimizes a contrastive multiple-instance learning objective that separates anomalous and normal representations without frame-level labels. To meet deployment constraints, an Adaptive Confidence Scheduler (ACS) dynamically skips low-information frames at inference time, reducing redundant computation in static scenes. Evaluated on UCF-Crime, ShanghaiTech, and CUHK Avenue, VigilFormer achieves AUC scores of 87.83%, 97.21%, and 89.74% respectively, at 41.5 FPS on a single GPU, outperforming recent weakly-supervised methods in both accuracy and speed.

</details>


### [5] [Interpolation between Convolution and Attention via K-Nearest Neighbors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14725)
*Mingi Kang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文提出ConvNN，将卷积与自注意力统一为“k近邻选择+加权聚合”的同一框架，显示二者位于同一连续谱系，可作为卷积或注意力的可替换层以探索局部到全局的中间形态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: CNN与Transformer在视觉中常被视为本质不同：CNN局部、注意力全局。作者认为两者核心都是“选择邻居并加权聚合”，差别仅在邻居选择准则（空间距离vs特征相似），因此希望建立统一理论与可实践框架，方便系统性探索两者之间连续过渡与设计空间。

Method: 提出Convolutional Nearest Neighbors (ConvNN)：以k近邻为基础的统一算子。- 邻居选择：可由归一化空间坐标（恢复标准/深度可分离卷积）或由缩放点积相似度（恢复自注意力及稀疏变体如KVT）。- 加权聚合：通过可配置核/权重函数对所选邻居加权求和。- 可插拔：作为卷积或注意力层的替代；可配置相似函数、kNN策略、位置编码、聚合核，在局部-全局之间连续调节。

Result: 在理论上严格“精确地”复现标准卷积、深度可分离卷积、自注意力及其稀疏变体；在工程上提供一个统一实现，可在同一模块内切换并探索中间设计（文摘未给具体数值性能）。

Conclusion: 卷积与自注意力并非截然不同，而是同一kNN聚合框架下的两端。ConvNN提供统一视角与可用算子，便于在局部与全局信息聚合之间进行系统化折中与扩展。

Abstract: The shift from Convolutional Neural Networks to Transformers has reshaped computer vision, yet these two architectural families are typically viewed as fundamentally distinct. Convolutional Neural Networks are defined by spatially local convolution operations, while Transformers rely on global self-attention. We argue that convolution and self-attention, despite their apparent differences, can be unified within a single k-nearest neighbor aggregation framework. The critical insight is that both operations are special cases of neighbor selection and weighted aggregation. Convolution selects neighbors by spatial proximity while self-attention selects by feature similarity, revealing that they lie on a continuous spectrum rather than representing categorically different computations.
  We introduce Convolutional Nearest Neighbors (ConvNN), a unified framework that formalizes this connection. ConvNN exactly recovers standard and depthwise convolution by restricting neighbor selection to normalized spatial coordinates, and exactly recovers self-attention and its sparse variants, including KVT-attention, by replacing spatial proximity with scaled dot-product similarity. Beyond these special cases, ConvNN serves as a drop-in replacement for both convolution and attention layers, enabling systematic exploration of the intermediate spectrum between local and global aggregation through configurable similarity functions, neighbor selection strategies, positional encodings, and aggregation kernels.

</details>


### [6] [FairGen: Preference-Aligned Diffusion for Demographically Equitable Medical Image Synthesis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14727)
*Zhimin Li,Ruichen Zhang,Zhen Tan,Howard J Aizenstein,Jingtong Hu,Tianlong Chen*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出FairGen：一种公平感知的扩散生成框架，用于合成在各人群间均衡且保持病理关键信息的医学影像，以缓解训练数据的人群失衡与诊断偏差问题。在皮肤科、放射科和神经影像任务上显著提升公平性，同时保持接近原始数据训练的诊断准确度，并通过临床专家评审与外部验证证明其泛化性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 临床影像数据常因医疗可及性差异与疾病在不同人群间的患病率/表型差异而高度不均衡；传统AI在此情境下易学习到偏置，导致对少数或稀有表型人群诊断性能下降，进一步放大医疗不公平。作者动机是通过数据生成弥补人群与表型覆盖不足，同时确保病理相关特征被真实保留并与临床偏好一致。

Method: 提出FairGen，一个融合扩散模型与“临床偏好对齐”的公平生成框架：在扩散合成过程中嵌入医生对病理显著性与人群覆盖的偏好信号，导向生成在各亚群间分布均衡且含病理判别特征的样本；随后将合成数据与原始临床数据结合训练下游分类器；并在皮肤、胸片、脑MRI基准上评估公平性与准确度，同时进行专家盲评与外部数据集验证。

Result: 在三项基准任务上，FairGen的公平性指标分别提升：皮肤图像95.9%、胸部X光80.0%、脑MRI 35.2%；同时保持与原始数据训练模型相当的诊断准确率。专家评审与独立队列外部验证显示改进并非仅限于分布内或单纯保真度指标。

Conclusion: 通过引入公平感知的扩散合成与临床偏好对齐，可在不显著牺牲准确度的情况下，系统性提升不同人群亚组的覆盖与诊断公平性；方法具有跨模态可迁移性并在外部数据上具备可推广性。

Abstract: Medical imaging is central to modern diagnostics, and artificial intelligence (AI) systems are increasingly used to support image-based analysis by improving efficiency, accuracy, and access to care. However, inequities in healthcare access and differential disease prevalence create severe demographic imbalances in clinical image data. Such imbalances are compounded by the fact that diseases can manifest with distinct features across demographic groups, rendering certain phenotypic presentations naturally rare. AI models trained on such imbalanced data risk perpetuating diagnostic bias and widening healthcare disparities. Here we introduce FairGen, a fairness-aware diffusion framework that synthesizes demographically balanced medical images while preserving pathology-relevant visual features. By embedding physician-aligned preferences into the generation process, FairGen improves subgroup coverage during synthesis and downstream classification. Applied to dermatology, radiology, and neuroimaging benchmark tasks, FairGen achieves fairness improvements of 95.9% for skin images, 80.0% for chest radiography, and 35.2% for brain MRI, while maintaining competitive diagnostic accuracy relative to models trained on original clinical data. Clinician-facing expert review and external validation on independent cohorts further support that these gains extend beyond standard fidelity metrics and are not confined to the original in-distribution datasets.

</details>


### [7] [FUSE: Quantifying Uncertainty in Vision-Language Models by Bayesian Fusing Epistemic and Aleatoric Uncertainty](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14728)
*Harry Zhang,Luca Carlone*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出FUSE框架，以贝叶斯方式融合嵌入级（杂讯/歧义）与模型级（认知）不确定性，得到单标量不确定性，能更好预测VLM输出正确性并实现SOTA校准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: VLM在机器人等高风险应用中需可靠不确定性评估；现有方法往往只刻画单一来源（数据噪声或模型不确定性），难以稳健预测输出正确性与做风险感知决策。

Method: 构建FUSE概率框架：1) 估计由视觉-语言歧义引起的“嵌入级”偶然不确定性（aleatoric）；2) 以语义响应多样性刻画VLM的“模型级”认知不确定性（epistemic）；3) 通过贝叶斯融合机制解析地合并两种不确定性，输出单一标量不确定性，用于置信度与正确性预测。

Result: 在多项基准上优于现有基线，取得最先进的不确定性校准性能，并能较可靠地预测模型输出是否正确。

Conclusion: 同时建模并贝叶斯融合数据与模型两类不确定性能显著提升VLM置信度与风险评估质量，适用于下游需要可靠决策的场景（如机器人）。

Abstract: Vision-language models (VLMs) are playing an increasingly important role across multiple domains. In many applications, such as robotics, it is crucial to quantify the uncertainty in the output of these models. } We develop FUSE, a probabilistic framework for capturing two complementary sources of uncertainty in vision-language modeling: (i) aleatoric embedding-level uncertainty derived from input data vision-language ambiguity, and (ii) epistemic model-level uncertainty estimated from the semantic response diversity of VLMs. Our approach formulates a Bayesian fusion mechanism that analytically combines these uncertainty sources to produce a scalar measure of uncertainty. This measure can be used to reliably predict the model's output correctness for downstream applications. We demonstrate that our method outperforms baselines and achieves SOTA uncertainty calibration.

</details>


### [8] [Hierarchical GRU with Input-Conditioned Slot Queries for Ball Action Anticipation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14730)
*Parthsarthi Rawat*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种分层模型，在30秒观测后预测接下来5秒内10类球权相关动作，融合局部Transformer、GRU与解码器并配稀有类别友好的匹配与高斯软目标，在SoccerNet基准测试达17.91% mAP。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有足球转播视频中的动作预判难点在于：事件稀疏且类别不均衡，时间定位不确定，且需要跨多尺度时序上下文；因此需要一种既能捕捉局部视觉线索又能聚合长时依赖、并能缓解类别不平衡与时间噪声的方法。

Method: 分层时序建模：1) 将30秒窗口划分为6个5秒子窗，使用共享的局部Transformer对每个子窗的片段级特征编码；2) 用GRU沿子窗聚合全局时间上下文；3) 用带K个输入条件事件槽的Transformer解码器，通过三头（目标性、类别、时间偏移）解码预测；4) 训练时引入频率重加权的Hungarian匹配以偏向稀有类，并用高斯软目标监督时间分箱。

Result: 在SoccerNet Ball Action Anticipation基准测试服务器上取得17.91% mAP。

Conclusion: 分层Transformer+GRU框架结合重加权匹配与软时间监督，可在转播视频中有效进行短期（5秒）球类动作预判，并对长尾类别更友好。

Abstract: We present a hierarchical model for ball action anticipation in football broadcast video. Given a 30-second observation window, the system predicts actions occurring in the subsequent 5-second window across 10 classes. A shared local Transformer encodes clip-level features within each 5-second sub-window; a GRU then aggregates temporal context across all sub-windows; finally, a Transformer decoder with K input-conditioned event slots decodes the anticipation target via three decoupled heads (objectness, class, temporal offset). We introduce frequency-reweighted Hungarian matching that systematically favours rare action classes, and Gaussian soft targets for temporal bin supervision. On the SoccerNet Ball Action Anticipation benchmark, our method achieves 17.91% mAP on the test server.

</details>


### [9] [BBR-Net: Boundary-Balanced Replay for Continual Medical Image Segmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14731)
*Zahid Ullah,Sieun Choi,Jihie Kim*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出BBR-Net，在连续学习的心脏超声分割中用边界感知与类均衡重放，显著减忘且接近离线联合训练；但当初始域结构噪声大时重放失效，说明结构信息质量比记忆容量更关键。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有重放方法多保留外观而未显式建模解剖结构，导致在域移位下易灾难性遗忘。作者检验“结构一致性是否支配知识保持”，并设计面向解剖边界的重放机制。

Method: 提出Boundary-Balanced Replay Network（BBR-Net）：(1) 边界感知优先级选择重放样本，聚焦解剖边界信息；(2) 类均衡采样，缓解类别不均；在CAMUS↔CardiacNet两种任务顺序上评测，并做消融与受控结构扰动实验（逐步腐化边界）。

Result: 前向（CAMUS→CardiacNet）中，BBR-Net源任务性能接近离线联合训练，显著降低遗忘且维持目标域适应；消融表明边界优先与类均衡结合能更好平衡保留与适应。反向（CardiacNet→CAMUS）中，若初始表征来自噪声高、结构不一致数据，结构感知重放失效。结构扰动实验显示，边界可靠性下降会单调增加遗忘。

Conclusion: 在医学分割的连续学习中，域移位下的知识保持关键在于解剖结构的可靠保存；重放机制需显式考虑结构可靠性，而不仅仅是扩大记忆容量。

Abstract: Continual learning for medical image segmentation remains challenging under domain shift because replay-based methods often preserve appearance information without explicitly modeling anatomical structure. This study investigates whether structural consistency governs knowledge retention in continual cardiac ultrasound segmentation. We propose the Boundary-Balanced Replay Network (BBR-Net), which selects replay samples using boundary-aware priority and class balance to preserve anatomically informative regions. The method is evaluated on CAMUS and CardiacNet under forward (CAMUS to CardiacNet) and reverse (CardiacNet to CAMUS) task orders. In the forward setting, BBR-Net retains source-task performance close to an offline joint-training reference, while markedly reducing catastrophic forgetting and preserving competitive target-task adaptation. Ablation results show that boundary-aware prioritization contributes to retention and improves the balance between source-task preservation and target-task adaptation when combined with class-aware sampling. In contrast, the reverse setting reveals that structure-aware replay fails when initial representations are learned from noisy and structurally inconsistent data. To isolate this effect, we conduct a controlled structural perturbation analysis by progressively corrupting source-task boundaries while keeping the dataset, architecture, and training protocol fixed. Forgetting increases consistently as structural reliability decreases, suggesting that replay effectiveness is strongly influenced by the quality of stored structural information, rather than by memory capacity alone. These findings indicate that preserving anatomical structure under domain shift is a central factor in continual medical image segmentation, and that replay mechanisms should account for structural reliability to support robust knowledge retention.

### [10] [Steady-Forcing: Balancing Spatial Persistence and Motion Continuity in Long-Horizon Nature Video Diffusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14732)
*Matiur Rahman Minar,Seunghun Oh,GangHyeon Jeong,Unsang Park*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出Steady-Forcing框架，缓解自回归视频扩散在长时段生成中的“稳定-运动”权衡：保持固定相机场景背景一致性的同时维持水火烟等流体现象的连贯运动。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自回归视频扩散在长时间滚动会出现两难：增强空间稳定性会抑制运动，导致自然流体停滞；而追求运动又会引入背景漂移。固定机位自然场景更易分离这两类失效，现有通用基准（如VBench）对这类问题惩罚不足，亟需方法与评测共同改进。

Method: 提出Steady-Forcing的记忆与训练框架，关键组件包括：1) 持久视觉锚V-Sink以固定背景；2) 指数滑动平均的运动记忆EMA-Sink以积累与延续运动；3) 分块相对时间编码以稳住长时依赖；4) 周期性缓存净化避免误差累积；5) 来自Wan2.1-14B教师的蒸馏，结合运动奖励先验与任务定制配置。

Result: 在七个基线之上，显著提升长时背景一致性与成像质量；盲测用户研究显示更强的稳定性与运动连续性感知。基准分析发现通用VBench对固定机位伪影惩罚不足，且将由漂移引起的光流误判为“动态度”，未直接惩罚纹理硬化或流动停滞。

Conclusion: Steady-Forcing在固定相机、长时自然流视频中同时保持背景身份与流体动态，缓解稳定-运动冲突；现有通用指标不充分，需建立面向静态机位自然流的任务特定评测。

Abstract: Autoregressive video diffusion models enable streaming generation but often degrade over long rollouts: static scene layouts drift, while mechanisms that improve spatial stability tend to suppress motion, causing natural flows such as water, fire, or smoke to stagnate. We study this stability-motion trade-off in fixed-camera long-horizon nature video generation, where the two failure modes can be more clearly separated than in moving-camera settings. We propose Steady-Forcing, a memory and training framework combining a persistent visual anchor (V-Sink), an exponential moving-average motion memory (EMA-Sink), block-relative temporal encoding, periodic cache purification, and distillation from a Wan2.1-14B teacher with motion-rewarded priors under task-focused configurations. Together, these components are designed to preserve background identity while sustaining visually plausible fluid dynamics over multi-minute autoregressive rollouts. Evaluations across seven baselines show that Steady-Forcing improves long horizon background consistency and imaging quality, while a blind user study indicates stronger perceived stability and motion continuity. The benchmark evaluation further suggest that generic VBench aggregate scores under-penalize fixed-camera artifacts as well as rewarding drift-induced optical flow as Dynamic Degree while not directly penalizing texture hardening or flow stagnation - motivating future task-specific benchmarks for static-camera nature-flow evaluation. Project page: https://minar09.github.io/steadyforcing/

</details>


### [11] [UtVAA: Ultra-tiny Vision Transformer with Affix Attention for Mobile Image Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14735)
*Romiyal George,Sathiyamohan Nishankar,Selvarajah Thuseethan,Roshan G. Ragel*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: UtVAA 提出一种面向移动/边缘设备的超小型 ViT，通过线性注意力与高效卷积组合，在<1M参数与低 FLOPs 下实现有竞争力的图像分类精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统 ViT 计算和参数量大，二次复杂度的自注意力和较重的主干限制了在资源受限设备上的部署。需要在不显著牺牲判别力的前提下，将 Transformer 重新设计为极小模型。

Method: 设计 UtVAA 架构：1) Affix Attention 模块融合三类表征：a) depthwise-pointwise 的局部特征提取；b) 线性自注意力以降低复杂度；c) 坐标注意力以建模空间依赖；并以轻量“三级融合”汇聚局部与全局信息。2) Dilated Bottleneck 利用扩张深度可分离卷积扩大感受野，辅以残差保证稳定优化与低 FLOPs。3) 提供 Tiny/Medium/Large 多尺度变体，最小模型仅约204.7K参数、53.95M FLOPs。

Result: 在 CIFAR-10/100、PlantVillage-Tomato、SLIF-Tomato 等数据集上，UtVAA 在<1M 参数范围内取得与现有方法相当或有竞争力的准确率。

Conclusion: Transformer 视觉模型可在严格算力预算下被重构为超小型架构而不显著损失判别性能，UtVAA 适合移动与边缘部署，并提供开源实现。

Abstract: Vision Transformers (ViTs) have demonstrated strong representation capability in image classification. However, their quadratic self-attention complexity and large parameter counts limit deployment on resource-constrained mobile and edge devices. This paper introduces UtVAA, an ultra-tiny Vision Transformer architecture designed for efficient visual recognition under strict computational budgets. It incorporates a novel Affix Attention block that combines depthwise-pointwise local feature extraction, linear self-attention, coordinate attention for spatial dependency modelling, and a lightweight ternary fusion strategy to integrate local and global representations. In addition, Dilated Bottleneck blocks expand the receptive field using dilated depthwise separable convolutions while maintaining low FLOPs and stable optimisation through residual connections. UtVAA is implemented in scalable Tiny, Medium, and Large variants, with the smallest model containing 204.67K parameters and 53.95M FLOPs. Experimental results on CIFAR-10, CIFAR-100, PlantVillage-Tomato and SLIF-Tomato datasets show that UtVAA achieves competitive accuracy within a sub-million-parameter regime. Overall, the results demonstrate that transformer-based vision models can be redesigned into ultra-tiny architectures without significant loss in discriminative performance, making UtVAA suitable for mobile and edge deployment. Code is available at https://github.com/romiyal/UtVAA

### [12] [GridVQA-X: A Framework for Evaluating Multimodal Explainability Methods](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14740)
*Sujay Belsare,Sudarshan Nikhil,Sushant Kumar,Ponnurangam Kumaraguru,Chirag Agarwal*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出GridVQA-X诊断框架，用合成闭域数据与成对模型评测多模态可解释性方法能否区分真实跨模态推理与表层捷径。结果显示主流方法未能做到。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有多模态可解释方法（MxAI）缺少能区分真实跨模态推理（如空间关系组合）与浅层跨模态捷径（如词袋式属性匹配）的可靠评估基准；自然数据缺乏带有“真因果/真解释”的标注，导致无法判断解释是否忠实。

Method: 构建GridVQA-X：在闭世界合成环境中生成问题、图像及“数学上保证唯一”的解释；并在同构架上训练两类对照模型：M_pure学习稳健的空间-关系推理，M_spur被结构性约束为依赖跨模态捷径。用该对照对作为严格测试台，要求解释器对两模型给出可区分的推理路径。

Result: 广泛使用的MxAI方法在此基准上无法区分M_pure与M_spur，对依赖捷径的模型给出与真正推理相似的解释，表明其未能捕捉真实跨模态协同且存在“编造/幻觉式”推理。

Conclusion: 需要新的评估与方法以确保解释忠实地反映跨模态交互；GridVQA-X提供了带有可验证真解释的诊断框架，揭示当前方法的失效模式，并为未来MxAI研究提供标准化测试平台。

Abstract: With the increasing development of Vision-Language Models, it becomes imperative that their predictions are readily explainable to relevant stakeholders. However, the field of explainability has not kept pace with the multimodal surge. While recent Multimodal Explainable AI (MxAI) methods generate explanations to attribute the interaction between different modalities, current evaluation protocols lack the ground truth required to distinguish between true cross-modal reasoning (e.g., spatial composition) and shallow cross-modal shortcuts (e.g., Bag-of-Words attribute matching). It remains unknown whether MxAI methods faithfully capture synergistic interactions or merely hallucinate reasoning on models acting as simple feature detectors. In this paper, we introduce GridVQA-X, the first diagnostic framework specifically designed to evaluate cross-modal explainability. Unlike natural datasets, GridVQA-X leverages a closed-world synthesis logic to generate unique, mathematically guaranteed explanations. We utilize this controlled environment to train paired ground-truth models on identical architectures: $M_{\text{pure}}$, which learns robust spatial-relational reasoning and $M_{\text{spur}}$, which is structurally forced to rely on cross-modal shortcuts. This behavioral divergence creates a rigorous testbed: a faithful explainer must report distinct reasoning pathways for each model. Our findings reveal that widely used methods fail to distinguish between models relying on genuine spatial-relational reasoning and those exploiting cross-modal shortcuts, highlighting a critical gap in capturing true cross-modal synergy and misrepresenting how multimodal models actually make decisions.

### [13] [HorusEye: Language as Dynamic Attention for Emergency Visual Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14741)
*Armel Yara*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出HorusEye：在应急视觉分析中将语言作为动态注意力；构建含退化条件的RefCOCO-Degraded基准，系统评测多种VLM在指代定位、语言反馈恢复、健康VQA与幻觉；发现语言反馈对性能提升强依赖模型，热成像下出现“热成像悖论”，且BLIP-2在退化下更易幻觉，不适宜应急部署。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1) 构建RefCOCO-Degraded：3811张基础图像×4种条件（干净、雾、烟、热），共15244图像；2) 设计四阶段评测：a) 视觉指代定位（grounding）；b) 迭代式语言反馈恢复（语言引导修正/再定位）；c) 健康相关VQA任务；d) 幻觉分析；3) 横向比较多种VLM（Gemini、Qwen2-VL、BLIP-2、LLaVA、Kosmos-2）；4) 分析裁剪策略在RGB与热成像下的差异与失效。

Result: 语言反馈的有效性强依赖具体模型：在热成像条件下，Gemini通过迭代语言反馈可提升47.3%，而Qwen2-VL在相同协议下降低5.1%；发现“热成像悖论”：在RGB上有效的裁剪策略在热图像上灾难性失败；BLIP-2在退化条件下幻觉率上升显著。

Conclusion: 语言作为动态注意力在应急退化场景中并非普适增益，需模型感知与语言交互机制协同设计；应避免将RGB有效策略直接迁移到热成像；BLIP-2不宜用于应急部署；未来应构建更稳健的跨模态反馈与退化鲁棒性方法与基准。

Abstract: We introduce HorusEye, Language as Dynamic Attention for Emergency Visual Analysis. Our investigation followed five stages. The first one is benchmarking RefCOCO-Degraded, a dataset of 15,244 images (3,811 base images x 4 conditions: Clean, Fog, Smoke and Thermal) with systematic visual degradation. Through four research questions, we evaluate multiple VLMs (Gemini, Qwen2-VL, BLIP-2, LLaVA, Kosmos-2) across visual grounding the second stage, language feedback recovery the third one, health VQA tasks the fourth, and hallucination analysis the final stage. Our key finding is that language feedback effectiveness is model-dependent: Gemini achieves +47.3% improvement in thermal conditions through iterative language feedback, while Qwen2-VL shows -5.1% degradation under the same protocol. We also identify the 'Thermal Paradox' where cropping strategies that improve RGB performance catastrophically fail in thermal imagery. Furthermore, BLIP-2 uniquely hallucinates more under degradation, making it unsuitable for emergency deployment

### [14] [Style-CCL: Content-Preserving Style Transfer via Curriculum Continual Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14746)
*Shiwen Zhang,Haoyuan Wang,Xianghao Zang,Haibin Huang,Chi Zhang,Xuelong Li*

TL;DR: 提出Style-CCL：一种多阶段课程式持续学习框架，配合双分支SC-DiT与大规模反向三元组数据合成，逐步从语义风格到纹理风格、从干净到合成数据训练，并用随机记忆复习避免遗忘，实现更好的风格相似度、内容一致性和美学质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1) 构建百万级反向三元组合成数据。2) 设计双分支SC-DiT：用独立ROPE位置编码与因果mask解耦风格与内容。3) 提出Style-CCL：分阶段课程式持续学习，按难度从语义(易)到纹理(难)、从干净到合成数据训练；各阶段采用随机记忆复习以缓解灾难性遗忘。

Conclusion: 通过分支解耦与课程式持续学习，既提升纹理风格学习又保持内容，实现高质量、保内容的风格迁移；多阶段训练与记忆复习有效避免语义风格“压制”和遗忘。

Abstract: Content-Preserving Style transfer, given content and style references, remains challenging for Diffusion Transformers (DiTs) due to entangled content and style features. With a reverse triplet synthesis pipeline to build a million-scale training set and a dual-branch Style-Content DiT (SC-DiT) that decouples style and content via separate ROPE embeddings and causal masking, we observe that such a one-stage training paradigm on mixed style categories causes semantic styles to dominate, hindering texture style learning, and harming content preservation. To address these issues, we propose Style-CCL, a Multi-Stage Curriculum Continual Learning framework that trains SC-DiT from semantic (easy) to texture (hard) styles, and from clean to synthetic data, with Random Memory Rehearsal across stages to avoid catastrophic forgetting. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our Style-CCL achieves state-of-the-art performance in three core metrics: style similarity, content consistency, and aesthetic quality.

Abstract: Recent advancements have significantly expanded the theoretical context windows of Multimodal Embedding Models (MEMs). However, larger context windows do not necessarily translate into effective comprehension and representation of long-context multimodal inputs, which remains a critical bottleneck for real-world deployment. To address the lack of systematic evaluation in this setting, we introduce MMLongEmbed, the first comprehensive benchmark for evaluating MEMs in long-context scenarios. MMLongEmbed comprises four retrieval tasks spanning multiple context-length ranges, covering text, document, and video modalities. Through extensive evaluation of state-of-the-art models, we find that current architectures rely heavily on superficial feature matching and struggle to capture deep semantic and structural dependencies. We further observe that performance degradation varies systematically with context length and key information placement. Moreover, models exhibit substantially different robustness to redundant contextual information across modalities. For reproducibility, the benchmark and code are publicly available.

### [16] [Is My Vision-Language Data in Your AI? Membership Inference Test (MINT) Demo 2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14748)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 模型训练数据往往不透明，难以验证某条数据是否进入训练集；监管与合规（如数据权益、隐私、版权）要求对训练数据可审计，因此需要通用、可扩展的成员推断测试框架与工具。

Method: 提出MINT的理论框架，并根据审计对象可获取的信息量设计多种体系结构（含MINT、aMINT、gMINT）。在黑盒/灰盒等不同可见性场景下，对输入样本进行成员推断测试；同时构建支持图像与文本的端到端网页平台，整合多技术栈以面向广泛模型进行审计。

Result: 在流行人脸识别模型、4个SOTA大语言模型，以及多种大规模图像与文本公开数据集上进行实验，成员检测准确率最高可达约90%，显示方法在多模态与多模型上的有效性。

Conclusion: MINT Demo 2证明成员推断框架在实际场景中可行，并通过统一平台为图像与文本模型提供可操作的审计工具，助力AI透明度并支撑新兴AI法规的合规需求。

Abstract: We present the Membership Inference Test (MINT) Demo 2, a framework designed to improve transparency in machine learning training processes. MINT is a technique for experimentally determining whether specific data were used during machine learning model training. We establish the theoretical framework and propose multiple architectures for MINT depending on the amount of information known about the models that are being audited. Experimental results using a popular face recognition model, 4 state-of-the-art LLMs, and multiple, diverse, and large-scale public image and text databases achieve promising accuracy levels in the detection of training data of up to 90%. Building on these results, we introduce a comprehensive web platform1 that expands these capabilities to image and text modalities. The platform integrates a diverse technological stack, including MINT, aMINT, and gMINT, allowing users to audit a wide range of models. This demonstrator aims to promote AI transparency and provides a practical tool to foster compliance with emerging AI regulations.

### [18] [X-Tokenizer: A Multimodal Action Tokenizer for Vision-Language-Action Pretraining](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14752)
*Xirui Kang,Yanpei Shi,Lucy Liang,Roy Gan,Dongxiu Liu,Pushi Zhang,Danpeng Chen,Xiaoyi Qin,Yinan Zheng,Jinliang Zheng,Hao Wang,Xianyuan Zhan,Hang Su*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出X-Tokenizer：把动作离散化从“压缩/重建”转为“语义接口”，用语义残差量化(SRQ)将粗语义与细重建解耦，作为冻结模块为VLA提供共享动作接口与表征塑形监督，在大规模轨迹上预训练，并在真实与仿真任务上超越基线（多模态落地与长时程分别+13.5%与+8.25%）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有动作tokenizer多为重建优化，虽保留几何细节但对上游视觉-语言语义监督弱，难以把通用多模态推理对齐到可执行的连续控制；且跨机械臂平台缺少统一动作接口。

Method: 设计轻量编码器–语义残差量化(SRQ)–解码器框架：残差量化首层用遮蔽动作建模(MAM)学习“离散动作语言”捕获粗运动意图；后续层保留为重建导向的残差以刻画细粒度控制。再以对比对齐到预训练基础模型表示、以及下一帧视觉-语言特征预测进行预训练。将单个冻结的X-Tokenizer接入混合离散-连续VLA，作为表征塑形的监督信号与跨机器人共享动作接口。

Result: 在240万条轨迹（20亿帧）上预训练后，单一冻结X-Tokenizer在真实机器人总体指标和RoboTwin 2.0仿真上取得强性能；在多模态语义落地与长时程任务上分别比FAST提升+13.5%与+8.25%。

Conclusion: 将动作tokenization定位为VLA的语义接口而非仅压缩，可通过SRQ把语义与细节解耦并与基础模型对齐，为多机器人共享与VLA预训练提供有效监督，带来显著性能提升。

Abstract: Modern Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models must bridge pretrained vision-language reasoning and precise continuous robot control. Existing action tokenizers discretize actions primarily for reconstruction, producing codes that preserve motion geometry but provide only weak semantic supervision to the backbone. We therefore formulate action tokenization not as mere compression, but as semantic interface learning between multimodal reasoning and executable control. To this end, we introduce X-Tokenizer, a lightweight encoder-Semantic Residual Quantization (SRQ)-decoder architecture that provides a shared action interface across diverse robotic arm embodiments. Its key component, SRQ, imposes an asymmetric structure on residual vector quantization: the first level is trained with Masked Action Modeling (MAM) to form a discrete action language that captures coarse motion intent, while deeper levels remain reconstruction-oriented residuals that preserve fine-grained details. To further align action tokens with multimodal semantics, X-Tokenizer is pretrained with contrastive alignment to the representation space of a pretrained foundation model and with next-frame vision-language feature prediction. Pretrained on 2.4M trajectories (2.0B action frames), a single frozen X-Tokenizer plugs into a mixed discrete-continuous VLA as a representation-shaping supervision signal. X-Tokenizer achieves top real-world aggregate and strong RoboTwin 2.0 simulation results. Outperforming FAST in multimodal grounding (+13.5%) and long-horizon tasks (+8.25), it shows that action tokenizers serve as semantic interfaces for VLA pretraining beyond mere action compression.

### [19] [Beyond Self-Attention: Sub-Quadratic Vision Transformers for Fast Image Captioning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14753)
*Chiradeep Ghosh,Dakshina Ranjan Kisku*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 用GMM软聚类取代ViT自注意力，将复杂度从O(n^2)降到O(nK)，并用GPT式解码器生成字幕；在Flickr30K上表现优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于Transformer的图像字幕方法存在两大痛点：1) 视觉局部特征表达不足；2) 自注意力计算成本随patch数二次增长，效率低。作者希望在不牺牲语义建模能力的前提下显著降低计算量并提升性能。

Method: 重构视觉Transformer：将标准自注意力替换为基于高斯混合模型(GMM)的概率Transformer。利用EM算法将相似图像patch软聚类到固定K个簇，注意力在簇级别而非全局pairwise计算，使复杂度由O(n^2)变为O(nK, K<<n)。上游视觉编码得到簇级表示，下游采用自回归GPT式文本解码器生成描述。

Result: 在Flickr30K数据集上进行评测，取得与现有方法相比具有竞争力且显著提升的结果（摘要未给出具体指标，但声称优于SOTA或主流基线）。

Conclusion: 基于GMM的聚类注意力可有效替代ViT中的全局自注意力，在保持/提升描述质量的同时大幅降低计算成本；说明软聚类的局部结构归纳偏置对图像字幕任务有益，并为高效视觉-语言建模提供了可行方向。

Abstract: Image captioning is a challenging and significant task that aims to generate coherent and semantically meaningful textual descriptions for given images. To accomplish this task, it requires a deep understanding of visual content along with the ability to express that understanding in natural language. Despite remarkable progress with transformer-based architectures, existing approaches often suffer from limitations, such as a lack of rich local feature representations and the high computational cost of quadratic self-attention. The proposed model focuses on improving computational efficiency by restructuring the vision transformer architecture. In designing this approach, the standard self-attention mechanism in Vision Transformers is replaced with a probabilistic transformer approach based on a Gaussian Mixture Model (GMM), a soft-clustering technique. Instead of computing pairwise attention among all image patches, the model groups similar patches into a fixed number of clusters using an Expectation-Maximization (EM) algorithm. This clustering-based mechanism reduces the computational complexity from quadratic O(n^2) to linear O(nK), where K << n. The autoregressive GPT-based decoder is used for caption generation. The model is evaluated on the Flickr 30K dataset, demonstrating competitive and significant improvement over existing works.

### [20] [Sub-Semantic Image Segmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14754)

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出“次语义”图像分割：介于纹理分割与语义分割之间，利用语言描述稳定外观模式并由SAM3落地为掩码；为此提出DETECTURE解决三类失效（语言泄漏、提示竞争、语义失真），并构建TextureADE数据集，实验优于多种基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统纹理分割只靠视觉线索，语义分割按对象命名；很多场景需要用语言描述细粒度的外观模式（如“粗糙木纹”“细密网格”），但不一定对应完整对象。现有VL+分割直接耦合不稳、易串扰，缺乏数据集评测。

Method: 将通用视觉-语言模型与可提示分割骨干SAM3耦合，并识别三类耦合失败：1）纹理区域间语言泄漏；2）在分割骨干内的多提示竞争；3）从语言到掩码接口的语义失真。DETECTURE提出相应机制抑制泄漏、解耦提示、校正接口映射；并构建从ADE20K派生的TextureADE用于训练/评估。

Result: 在多个数据集与多种指标上，DETECTURE相较多种基线取得最强或一致领先的性能，展示更稳定、可控的基于语言的次语义分割能力。

Conclusion: 次语义分割填补纹理与语义分割之间的空白。DETECTURE通过解决三大失效实现鲁棒的语言到纹理模式落地；TextureADE为该方向提供标准化数据。代码公开，便于复现与扩展。

Abstract: Images can be segmented based on visual cues (i.e., texture segmentation) or into objects (i.e., semantic segmentation). We propose a new category of sub-semantic image segmentation that blurs the line between the two. In sub-semantic image segmentation, language is not used to name whole objects. Instead, it is used to partition an image into stable appearance patterns that can be described by language. To do that, we couple a general-purpose vision-language model to SAM 3, a promptable segmentation backbone whose native text pathway can ground rich descriptions into masks. Simple coupling fails for a number of reasons that we identify in the paper, and we overcome them by introducing DETECTURE that resolves three concrete failure modes -- language leakage between texture regions, prompt competition inside the segmentation backbone, and semantic distortion at the language-to-mask interface. Since there is no dataset of sub-semantic image segmentation, we introduce one, termed TextureADE. The new dataset is derived from the ADE20K dataset using a system we designed. We compare DETECTURE to a number of baselines and find that it achieves the strongest performance on several datasets using different metrics. Code is available at https://github.com/Scientific-Computing-Lab/TextureDetecture.

### [21] [Where Does Texture Evidence Live in SAM? Features, Proposal Masks, and Texture Segmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14755)
*Nadav Orenstein,Aviad Cohen Zada,Shai Avidan,Gal Oren*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文探讨冻结的SAM在纹理分割任务中的潜在证据：默认不擅长，但并非“纹理盲”；多尺度特征保留纹理组织，proposal库常含纹理对齐的掩码/碎片。自然场景多需“拼装+决策”，合成场景多为“选择现有”。失败应分解为表示证据、proposal支持、读出失配与承诺失败。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有SAM偏向目标/物体中心的分割，在以材料或重复外观定义区域的纹理分割上易失败。该失败成因不明：是缺乏纹理表征、proposal缺失，还是读出策略错误？在不微调SAM的前提下，厘清其内部已保留的纹理相关证据，有助于理解能力边界与设计更高效的读出/适配策略。

Method: 完全冻结SAM（不微调主干、不重训proposal生成器），考察两类“证据空间”：1）多尺度特征，用最小化聚类读出进行探针；2）自动proposal库，将其视为监督整合的证据来源。跨多个数据组（RWTD、STLD、从ADE20K精选的精裁补充集、以及用ControlNet拼接的PTD桥接档案）评估，分析默认mask失败的成分。

Result: 冻结SAM默认不是纹理分割器，但并非完全缺乏纹理信息：粗粒度特征仍保留纹理组织；proposal库中经常包含与纹理对齐的掩码或片段。自然场景更常需要将碎片组装并在竞争区域间做出承诺；较干净的合成场景则常可直接选择已连贯的proposal即可。

Conclusion: 应将默认掩码失败拆解为四类：表示层面的证据、proposal库支持度、读出（readout）方式不匹配、以及最终“承诺”决策失败。改进纹理分割不必首先微调 backbone，而可优先优化读出与proposal整合策略；在复杂自然图像中尤其需面向“碎片组装+承诺”的机制。

Abstract: Texture segmentation stresses foundation segmentation because meaningful regions are defined by material or repeated appearance rather than object identity. Segment Anything Models (SAMs) often fail by default on such texture-defined partitions, but this failure is ambiguous: the texture evidence may be absent, missing from the proposal bank, or present but selected or assembled incorrectly by an object-centric readout. We ask what texture-relevant evidence is already preserved in frozen SAM before adaptation. We study two frozen evidence spaces: multiscale features, probed with a minimal clustering readout, and the automatic proposal bank, treated as evidence for a supervised consolidation readout. SAM is frozen throughout; we do not fine-tune the backbone or retrain the proposal generator. Across RWTD, STLD, an ADE20K-selected refined-crop complement, and a ControlNet-stitched PTD bridge archive, frozen SAM is not a texture segmenter by default, but its failures are not simple texture blindness. Coarse frozen features preserve texture organization, and proposal banks often contain texture-aligned masks or fragments. Natural scenes more often require assembly and commitment over fragments, while cleaner synthetic cases more often reduce to selecting an already coherent proposal. Default mask failure should therefore be decomposed into representation evidence, proposal-bank support, readout mismatch, and commitment failure.

</details>


### [22] [Divide-and-Denoise: A Game-Theoretic Method for Fairly Composing Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14756)
*Abhi Gupta,Polina Barabanshchikova,Vikas Garg,Samuel Kaski,Tommi Jaakkola*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出“Divide-and-Denoise（分配-去噪）”，在采样阶段协调多预训练扩散模型，通过公平分工与区域对齐，使各模型在其擅长的局部负责去噪，提升组合生成质量并减少缺失物体与属性不匹配。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多扩散模型组合常出现“一家独大”或模型互相冲突，导致条件生成中对象缺失、属性错配等。需要一种在不重训的前提下，于采样时协调各模型的机制，既公平又高效地利用各自专长。

Method: 定义“分配（allocation）”以指定每个模型对噪声样本各区域的责任；在每个时间步进行两步：(i) 通过“公平分割博弈”更新分配，最大化总体效用并满足公平性约束，将样本划分为若干区域；(ii) 依据分配对齐各模型，仅在被指派区域执行去噪，引导产生新的复合去噪过程，使分割与去噪并行演化。

Result: 在条件图像生成任务上，包含 GenEval 基准在内的多项指标优于基线，显著缓解了常见失败（如对象缺失、属性不匹配），并体现各模型专长被利用且无被忽视。

Conclusion: Divide-and-Denoise在无需再训练的前提下，为多扩散模型提供了动态公平分工与区域对齐的采样机制，提升组合生成的稳定性与质量，并有效协调模型间的竞争与冲突。

Abstract: The abundance of pre-trained diffusion models provides an opportunity for composition. Combining several models, however, runs the risk of one model dominating or models disagreeing with each other. Here, we propose Divide-and-Denoise, a method for coordinating multiple pre-trained diffusion models during sampling. Much like managing a specialized workforce, our method creates a fair but efficient division of labor across models. Central to our method is the notion of an allocation which defines the responsibility of each model to every region of the noisy sample. At every timestep, we then denoise by (i) updating the allocation by solving a fair division game, where we divide the sample into regions that maximize total utility under fairness constraints, and (ii) aligning the models with this allocation, where we guide each model to denoise within its assigned region. This leads to a new composite denoising process that evolves in tandem with a division process. We evaluate Divide-and-Denoise on conditional image generation. Across several quality metrics, including the GenEval benchmark, our method outperforms baselines and resolves common failures including missing objects and mismatched attributes. Experiments show that Divide-and-Denoise utilizes each model's expertise without neglecting any other model.

</details>


### [23] [Spatial Priors via Space Filling Curves for Small and Limited Data Vision Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14757)
*Leyla Naz Candogan,Arshia Afzal,Pol Puigdemont,Volkan Cevher*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出VIOLIN：用空间填充曲线(SFC)生成轻量掩码，向ViT注意力注入空间归纳偏置，几乎零参数/计算开销，在小模型与小数据上显著提升表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ViT注意力对输入置换等变，缺乏显式空间结构偏置；当模型容量小或数据有限时，性能受限。需要一种既高效又通用的方式在注意力中编码空间关系。

Method: 以多条空间填充曲线(Hilbert/蛇形等)扫描图像，为每条曲线构建位置随距离衰减的掩码；将多曲线掩码融合后与注意力矩阵逐元素相乘，形成带空间偏置的“遮罩注意力”。该机制参数增加<0.0015%，计算开销可忽略，可与LoRA等高效微调结合，并可用于预训练阶段。

Result: 在多项评测中稳定增益：VTAB-1K小数据微调全任务组提升，对强依赖空间信息的任务最高+8.7%；与LoRA叠加进一步提升；在ImageNet-1K上改进小型ViT架构（DeiT、DINO）预训练表现；在像素级CIFAR-100训练上最高+7.2%。

Conclusion: VIOLIN以极低成本为ViT注入空间归纳偏置，尤其在小模型与数据受限场景显著有效，通用于微调与预训练并可与参数高效方法互补。

Abstract: Though Vision Transformers (ViTs) have become the dominant backbone in many computer vision tasks, due to permutation equivariance, their attention mechanism lacks explicit spatial inductive biases. This become particularly important in two settings: when model capacity is small or training data is limited. Inspired by the attention masking strategies in Linear Transformers and the scanning patterns of Vision SSMs, we introduce VIOLIN, a lightweight masked attention mechanism that encodes spatial structure within attention via Space Filling Curves (SFCs) with less than 0.0015% extra parameters and negligible computational overhead. VIOLIN scans the image using multiple SFCs to construct curve-specific decay masks, which are then combined and multiplied with the attention matrix. Across a wide range of evaluations, VIOLIN consistently improves performance. In limited data regimes such as fine-tuning on VTAB-1K, it boosts accuracy across all task groups and by up to 8.7% on the tasks where spatial information is essential. It can be combined with parameter-efficient fine-tuning methods such as LoRA to further increase the performance. Beyond fine-tuning, VIOLIN improves various small scale ViT architectures (e.g., DeiT, DINO) during pretraining on ImageNet-1K. Additionally, on pixel-level CIFAR-100 training, a task that is highly dependent on location information, VIOLIN increases accuracy by up to 7.2%. Overall, VIOLIN provides a computationally efficient yet effective way to inject spatial inductive bias into ViTs, especially benefiting small models and limited data settings.

</details>


### [24] [Disentangling Hallucinations: Orthogonal Semantic Projection for Robust Interpretability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14758)
*Emirhan Bilgiç,Baptiste Caramiaux,Zhi Yan,Gianni Franchi*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文提出线性语义泄露导致多模态解释出现“语义幻觉”，并给出统一理论LSA与几何干预OSP，通过将查询向量与干扰概念正交化来降低幻觉、保持正确提示的忠实度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: VLM在安全关键场景中需要可信解释，但现有XAI方法会在错误文本提示下仍高亮显著图像区域（语义幻觉）。缺乏对这种现象及CLIP嵌入的形式化分析。

Method: 提出线性语义归因（LSA）理论框架，解释在高维嵌入中由线性语义泄露导致的普适现象；基于OMP残差性质，设计正交语义投影（OSP）对查询向量进行与干扰概念的正交化，剥离共享特征，仅保留独特语义信号；给出理论证明与实证评估。

Result: 理论上证明OSP能最小化幻觉，使归因对共享特征“盲化”；实验表明在多种判别式方法和VLM上，OSP降低错误提示下的显著高亮，同时对正确提示保持或提升忠实度。

Conclusion: 语义幻觉并非特定架构问题，而是高维线性嵌入中的内在属性；LSA提供统一视角，OSP作为简单几何干预有效缓解幻觉并维持解释可靠性。

Abstract: As Vision-Language Models are increasingly deployed in safety-critical applications, the trustworthiness of their explanations becomes crucial. Explainable AI (XAI) methods for Vision-Language Models often suffer from semantic hallucination, where attribution maps highlight prominent image regions even when prompted with incorrect text descriptions (e.g., highlighting a dog when prompted ``cat''). Although this problem is widespread, a formal mathematical analysis of XAI methods and CLIP embeddings is largely missing in the literature. We demonstrate that this phenomenon is not specific to a single architecture but is a fundamental consequence of Linear Semantic Leakage in high-dimensional embedding spaces. We propose a unified theoretical framework, Linear Semantic Attribution (LSA), which generalizes across discriminative methods. We introduce OSP, a geometric intervention that utilizes the residual property of OMP to disentangle unique semantic signals from shared concepts. We prove theoretically and demonstrate empirically that OSP minimizes hallucination by orthogonalizing the query vector against distractor concepts, rendering the attribution model blind to shared features while preserving fidelity for correct prompts. Our code is available at: https://github.com/emirhanbilgic/Orthogonal-Semantic-Projection

</details>


### [25] [Temporally Consistent and Controllable Video Generation of 2D Cine CMR via Latent Space Motion Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14759)
*Yiheng Cao,Gustavo Andrade-Miranda,Jiatian Zhang,Guillaume Sallé,Xin Gao*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种文本到视频生成框架，分离心脏的空间解剖与时间运动：先用微调扩散模型从临床文本生成首帧控制解剖，再用条件潜在流模型根据心动周期相位生成整段运动，保证时空一致。实现高时序相干与提示对齐，FID 31.68、CLIP 31.04，助力缓解医学数据稀缺。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 公共心脏磁共振（cine CMR）序列数据稀缺，限制了数据驱动方法（如深度学习）在心功能评估中的发展与泛化。需要一种能在保持解剖正确、运动连贯与病理多样性的前提下，按需生成高保真医学序列的数据合成方法。

Method: 文本到视频的两阶段解耦生成：1）空间解剖控制：对扩散模型进行微调，从临床文本提示生成起始帧，锁定解剖与病理特征；2）时间运动建模：构建以心动相位嵌入为条件的潜在流（latent flow）模型，从首帧出发生成完整心动周期，使空间结构在时间上保持一致并可控相位进程；整体保证时序相干与语义对齐。

Result: 模型可生成解剖与病理表现多样的cine CMR序列，具备高时间连贯与对提示的强保真；量化上，图像真实感FID=31.68，文图对齐CLIP=31.04。

Conclusion: 该解耦式文本到视频生成框架能按需合成高保真的心脏视频数据，兼顾解剖一致与时序控制，为缓解医学影像数据稀缺、促进下游心功能评估与研究提供可扩展途径。

Abstract: Cine cardiac magnetic resonance is the gold standard for assessing cardiac function, but the scarcity of public datasets limits the development of advanced data-driven models. To address this limitation, we propose a generative method for synthesizing temporally coherent and anatomically consistent cardiac sequences. Our text-to-video framework decouples cardiac spatial structure from temporal motion. First, a fine-tuned diffusion model synthesizes an initial frame from a clinical text prompt, controlling anatomical features. Then, a latent flow model conditioned on a cardiac phase embedding generates the complete cardiac motion, ensuring spatial consistency and temporal control. Our model generates anatomically and pathologically diverse sequences with high temporal coherence and strong fidelity to input prompts, achieving a FID of 31.68 for image realism and a CLIP score of 31.04 for text-image alignment. These experimental results highlight its potential to produce high-fidelity, on-demand medical data, offering a scalable solution to data scarcity.

### [26] [GeoRoPE: Ground-Aware Rotary Adaptation for Remote Sensing Foundation Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14760)
*Yu Luo,Kun Hu,Mengwei He,Xiaogang Zhu,Shan Zeng,Allen Benter,Wei Xiang,Patrick Filippi,Thomas Francis Bishop,Zhiyong Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出GeoRoPE，一种与RoPE兼容、参数高效的地理感知位置编码适配方法，解决多传感器/多分辨率遥感基础模型下的尺度不匹配与场景依赖的空间敏感度问题，提升跨分辨率鲁棒性与尺度敏感表征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 遥感基础模型常在多传感器、多地面采样距离(GSD)数据上预训练，但下游适配时仍存在尺度错配：同一token网格位移在不同传感器上对应不同地面距离，导致基于网格的位置先验在物理上不一致；且同一GSD下，不同场景（紧凑城市 vs. 同质景观）对位置敏感度需求不同。需一种既保留预训练先验、又能地理感知地校正位置编码的方法。

Method: 在冻结RSFM空间先验的前提下，通过轻量适配器注入GeoRoPE，对token级相对位置交互进行双重校准：1) Geo-Coordinate Calibration (GCC)：按单步token网格代表的实际地面距离重标定相对坐标，实现跨GSD的一致地理坐标；2) Geo-Frequency Calibration (GFC)：对RoPE的基础频率施加与关系相关的缩放因子，使位置敏感度可随场景空间粒度自适应调整。整体与RoPE兼容、参数高效。

Result: 在多种RSFM、传感器、分辨率与下游任务上，GeoRoPE带来更好的跨分辨率鲁棒性与更强的尺度敏感表征能力，较基线有一致提升。

Conclusion: 仅靠多传感器/多GSD预训练不足以解决尺度错配。通过对相对坐标与频率的地理感知校准，GeoRoPE能在不破坏原有先验的前提下提供物理一致、场景自适应的位置编码，实证上提升多任务与多分辨率表现。

Abstract: Remote-sensing foundation models (RSFMs) benefit from pretraining on imagery from multiple sensors and ground sampling distances (GSDs), but such exposure alone does not resolve scale mismatch during downstream adaptation. A fixed token-grid offset can correspond to different ground distances across sensors, making grid-based positional priors physically inconsistent. Meanwhile, heterogeneous spatial granularity means that compact urban regions and homogeneous landscapes may require different positional sensitivities even under the same GSD. Therefore, we propose {GeoRoPE}, a ground-aware, RoPE-compatible, and parameter-efficient spatial adaptation method for RSFMs. GeoRoPE recalibrates token-level positional interactions from two complementary aspects. First, \textit{Geo-Coordinate Calibration (GCC)} rescales raw token-grid offsets according to the ground distance represented by one token-grid step, producing geo-calibrated relative coordinates across GSDs. Second, \textit{Geo-Frequency Calibration (GFC)} adjusts the native RoPE frequency with a relation-specific factor, enabling position sensitive adaptation to scene-dependent spatial granularity. GeoRoPE is injected into pretrained RSFMs through a lightweight adapter, preserving the frozen spatial prior while adding geo-aware positional corrections. Experiments across multiple RSFMs, sensors, resolutions, and downstream tasks demonstrate that GeoRoPE improves cross-resolution robustness and scale-sensitive representation learning.

</details>

Method: 两阶段思想中的第一阶段：对视频转录进行微观索引——(1)全局转录分析；(2)逐句分析；(3)用LLM作为评审依据语义相似度对句子分组。为保持上下文连贯性，在句子级评估提示中注入全局分析结果与相邻句信息。随后将这些分组用于语义分块与匹配的可视化（相关性热力图）。

Although many existing AI programs provide high-level video summaries based on AI-generated transcripts \cite{2,3,4,5}, these approaches are often limited to coarse overviews and lack detailed analysis of a video's structure, thematic progression, and semantic relationships, all of which are required for comprehensive video analysis.
  This paper proposes an LLM-based video summarization framework that balances macro-level comprehension with micro-level semantic analysis \cite{6,12,13}. The first stage of the process indexes the video at a micro level by (1) analyzing the full transcript, (2) analyzing individual transcript sentences, and (3) grouping these sentences by semantic similarity using an LLM as a judge \cite{6,13}. Contextual continuity is retained during sentence-level processing by incorporating both the global transcript analysis and adjacent sentence information into each evaluation prompt.
  This framework establishes a foundation for video analysis tools that visualize semantic chunking and semantic matching through relevance-based heatmaps. Limitations and future expansions of the framework are also discussed.

*Ishant Shanu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出在分配格（distributive lattice）上直接最小化次模函数的通用框架，避免将问题扩展到布尔格导致的指数级空间膨胀，并可复用已有布尔格上的SFM算法，大幅加速。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多计算机视觉与机器学习任务需要在分配格上进行次模函数最小化。现有主流做法是把函数外推到布尔格再优化，但这会把搜索空间指数扩张，导致优化极其低效，运行时间过长。需要一种在原分配格内工作的高效方法。

Method: 提出一个仅在分配格内部运作的通用框架：通过构造使布尔格SFM算法可被复用的表示/接口，将分配格上的问题等价地映射为在同一格内可处理的形式，避免到布尔格的外推与空间膨胀。框架兼容现有布尔格SFM算法作为黑箱调用。

Result: 在实验中，相比传统将分配格问题扩展到布尔格的做法，运行时间显著缩短（“巨大提升”）。

Conclusion: 在不扩大搜索空间的前提下，实现了对分配格上次模函数的高效最小化，并能直接复用成熟的布尔格SFM算法，实践中显著加速，表明这是处理分配格SFM更可行的路径。

Abstract: Submodular function minimization has gained a lot of interest in recent years. They are highly applicable in the area of Computer Vision and Machine Learning. Often such applications require to work with submodular functions defined on distributive lattice. Current best way of dealing with it is using a transformation which extrapolates the submodular function for the respective boolean lattice. It makes optimization system too inefficient due to enlargement of the working space. Quantitatively, the expanded space has additional exponential (in set size) number of elements. We propose a generic framework for dealing with distributive lattice which only works within distributive lattice. Our framework allows one to use already established submodular function minimization algorithms for boolean lattice. In our experiment, we show the huge improvement in terms of running time over tranditional methods for handling distributive lattice.

### [29] [Momentum-Guided Semantic Forecasting (MoFore) for Self-Supervised Video Representation Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14765)
*Qinwu Xu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出MoFore：通过预测未来潜在嵌入而非像素重建或标签对齐，进行自监督视频表征学习；引入随机时间间隔预测与对比正则，提升时序稳健与避免坍塌；在UCF101上表现出强时序一致性与语义结构，无需动作标签。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自监督视频学习多依赖：1) 重建（MAE/VideoMAE）侧重像素级恢复，可能与高层语义偏离；2) 对比/对齐（如CLIP）需跨模态或特定任务信号。需要一种既捕获长程时序动态、又不依赖像素重建或外部标签/对齐信号的方法。

Method: 提出Momentum-Guided Semantic Forecasting (MoFore)：以相隔较远的上下文片段为条件，预测未来片段的潜在表示（而非像素）。训练时采用随机化时间间隔的预测任务以增强跨时间尺度鲁棒性；并加入对比式正则，鼓励时间一致性、抑制表征坍塌。整体为自监督框架，无需动作标签。

Result: 在UCF101上，无监督预训练后表征展现：1) 定量上强时序稳定性；2) 学到的嵌入空间出现类别级结构；3) 定性检索显示对运动模式的感知与跨活动的有序组织。表明长程潜在预测可高效学习语义与时序兼顾的表征。

Conclusion: 长距离潜在表示预测结合对比正则，是一种无需重建目标的高效自监督视频学习范式；它能产生时序一致且语义有意义的表征，具备良好的跨时间尺度鲁棒性与计算效率。

Abstract: Self-supervised video representation learning has recently advanced through contrastive learning, masked reconstruction, and predictive representation learning. Reconstruction-based approaches such as MAE and VideoMAE learn representations by recovering masked visual content \cite{he2022mae,tong2022videomae}, while contrastive methods such as CLIP learn semantically meaningful embedding spaces through representation alignment \cite{radford2021clip}.
  In this work, we introduce a Momentum-Guided Semantic Forecasting framework (MoFore) for self-supervised video representation learning. Instead of optimizing for pixel-level reconstruction or task-specific semantic alignment, the proposed method learns temporally predictive video representations by forecasting future latent embeddings from temporally distant context clips. To improve robustness across temporal scales, we further introduce randomized temporal-gap forecasting during training. The framework combines predictive latent forecasting with contrastive regularization to encourage temporal consistency while preventing representation collapse.
  Experiments on the UCF101 dataset demonstrate that the proposed framework learns temporally consistent and semantically meaningful video representations without using action labels during training. Quantitative analysis shows strong temporal stability and emergent category-level structure in the learned embedding space, while qualitative retrieval experiments reveal motion-aware organization across related activities. Overall, the results suggest that long-range latent forecasting provides an effective and computationally efficient approach for self-supervised video representation learning without relying on reconstruction-based objectives.

This paper presents XMedFusion, a modular AI framework designed as an intelligent perception and reasoning module for autonomous medical systems. The proposed framework decomposes visual information into coordinated functional components that emulate expert-driven analysis, including a visual perception agent that extracts image-grounded evidence, a knowledge graph construction agent that structures clinically relevant findings, and a retrieval-guided drafting process that ensures a consistent reporting structure. A synthesis agent iteratively integrates visual and structured evidence through reasoning-driven verification to produce reliable and interpretable diagnostic outputs. ### [31] [An Empirical Analysis of Optimization Dynamics and Sparsity Boundaries in Large-Scale Pedestrian Attribute Recognition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14770)
*Houssam El Mir*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出在极端类别不平衡的行人属性识别中，用多标签Focal Loss（α=0.5, γ=2.0）在ResNet-18上可与BCE基线宏F1持平（62.32%），保持更好的难例挖掘与收敛；但当正例比例低于0.1%时出现“稀疏墙”，全局重加权失效，需实例级干预。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 合并PETA与PA-100K后形成10.9万图像多标签数据集，少数属性正例低至<1%。标准BCE在此极端不平衡下倾向压制稀有属性（“多数负类作弊陷阱”），影响取证检索/再识别中的属性召回。

Method: 以ResNet-18为骨干，系统消融多标签Focal Loss超参α与γ，比较与BCE在宏F1、难例挖掘与收敛动态方面的表现；方法仅改变损失函数，无额外计算开销，适合边缘部署。

Result: 在校准配置α=0.50、γ=2.0时，宏F1=62.32%，与BCE基线相当，同时展现更优的难例挖掘与更稳定的收敛过程。

Conclusion: 纯损失工程可在不增加计算的情况下缓解多数负类陷阱，但当正例占比<0.1%跨越“稀疏墙”后，全局重加权（如Focal Loss）不足以奏效，需转向实例级方法（如样本选择/重采样、对比学习、元学习或自适应阈值）。

Abstract: Pedestrian Attribute Recognition (PAR) is critical for video surveillance, enabling forensic search and re-identification systems. Extreme class imbalance remains a fundamental obstacle when merging PETA and PA-100K into a 109,000-image composite corpus, where minority attributes have positive sample fractions below 1%. This causes standard BCE optimization to suppress rare traits, a phenomenon we term the majority negative class cheating trap. We present a systematic ablation of Multi-Label Focal Loss hyperparameters (alpha and gamma) on a ResNet-18 backbone. A calibrated configuration (alpha=0.50, gamma=2.0) achieves a Macro F1-score of 62.32%, matching BCE baseline while preserving superior hard-example mining and convergence dynamics. Our approach uses pure loss-function engineering with zero computational overhead for edge deployment. We identify the Sparsity Wall, a hard boundary where positive sample fractions below 0.1% make global loss reweighting ineffective, requiring instance-level intervention.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有户外EQA常在目标进入视野即停止，无法进行证据导向的细粒度视角微调，难以回答需要更精确证据的自然语言问题。

Method: 1) 构建FG-EQA基准：含4万+仿真轨迹与1千真实轨迹，强调主动探索与细粒度视角调整。2) 提出ScoutVLA：受侦察蜂“摆尾舞”启发的证据驱动VLA。采用解耦双专家架构：视觉-语言专家负责语义意图推断与缺失证据定位；独立动作专家用高自由度flow matching生成连续的视角精炼轨迹。3) 解耦训练与知识绝缘：阻隔动作梯度破坏多模态推理，平衡连续控制与语义推理。

Result: 在模拟与真实场景中优于SOTA：平均严格成功率提高10.48×，问答正确率提高7.72×；并展示了更稳健的证据寻访与视角精炼能力。

Conclusion: 细粒度主动感知对于户外EQA至关重要。通过解耦的语义-动作专家与知识绝缘训练策略，ScoutVLA在FG-EQA上实现显著性能提升，验证了“证据驱动、迭代勘察”的有效性。

Abstract: Aerial Embodied Question Answering (EQA) requires Unmanned Aerial Vehicles (UAVs) to actively perceive the environment and answer natural language questions. Existing outdoor EQA systems usually stop once the target enters the UAV's field of view, leaving the fine-grained viewpoint adjustment needed for evidence-seeking questions largely unresolved. To address this issue, we introduce FG-EQA, a fine-grained active perception EQA benchmark with more than 40K simulated trajectories and 1K real-world trajectories. Drawing inspiration from the ``waggle dance'' of scout bees, which iteratively adjust their flight paths to verify target information, we propose ScoutVLA, an evidence-driven Vision-Language-Action model for outdoor EQA. To emulate this active exploration behavior, ScoutVLA features a decoupled dual-expert architecture: a vision-language expert infers the semantic intent to identify missing evidence, while an independent action expert employs high-DoF flow matching to generate continuous viewpoint-refinement trajectories. To balance the competing demands of continuous control and semantic reasoning, we devise a decoupled training strategy with a knowledge insulation mechanism that prevents the action gradients from erasing the model's multimodal reasoning ability. Extensive simulated experiments and a qualitative real-world field study both verify the superiority of ScoutVLA over the state-of-the-art baselines, demonstrating a 10.48$\boldsymbol{\times}$ higher average strict success rate and a 7.72$\boldsymbol{\times}$ higher average QA correctness.

</details>


### [33] [Double-Helix Vision (DH-V2): A Geometry-Based Visual Sampler for Bandwidth-Constrained Perception](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14773)
*Jinwen Wen*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出Double-Helix Vision (DH)，用两条黄金比例启发的相位相反螺旋在2D图像上进行仿生中心凹采样，将图像压缩为紧凑1D信号；在极低采样下仍能保持几何结构，并以CPU在毫秒内完成感知流水线，无需神经网络。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统视觉需均匀处理全部像素，计算/带宽开销大且在资源受限平台不友好；随机稀疏采样难以保持场景几何结构与时空一致性。作者动机是用几何先验与仿生采样在极低采样率下仍保留结构信息，并提供可用于机器人快速感知的轻量流水线。

Method: 设计两条相位差180度的对偶螺旋(Alpha/Beta)在图像平面采样，中心高密、边缘稀疏；将2D图像映射为1D序列。围绕该采样构建CPU友好的流水线：空间映射、时间上的碰撞检测、帧内结构视差估计；提供JSON可序列化的API输出感知报告。无NN依赖。

Result: 在4K图像上实现约1433×压缩(减少99.93%)且仍保持场景几何结构；在1080p上整条流水线仅0.52 ms (CPU-only)；在CIFAR-10极限采样预算(K=每条螺旋128点)下，相比均匀随机采样分类准确率提升+6.03%；API报告约2.7 KB，子毫秒级输出。

Conclusion: 几何驱动的双螺旋采样在极低采样率下兼顾结构保持与实时性，为资源受限设备与机器人提供无需深度网络的快速感知方案；显示在分类与时空感知任务上的初步优势，并以开源实现支撑。

Abstract: We present Double-Helix Vision (DH), a geometry-based visual sampler that compresses 2D images into compact 1D signals using paired golden-ratio-inspired spiral trajectories. Rather than processing every pixel uniformly, DH employs two phase-shifted helices (Alpha and Beta, offset by 180 degrees) to sample the image with biologically-inspired foveation: high density at the center, sparse coverage at the periphery. At 4K resolution, DH achieves a 1,433x compression ratio (99.93% reduction) while preserving the geometric structure of the scene. The full perception pipeline -- including spatial mapping, temporal collision detection, and intra-frame structural disparity estimation -- runs in 0.52 ms at 1080p on CPU-only hardware, with no neural network dependencies. On CIFAR-10 at extreme sampling budgets (K=128 points per helix), DH achieves a +6.03% accuracy gain over uniform random sampling. A JSON-serializable Robotics API is provided, delivering sub-millisecond spatial perception reports in 2.7 KB packets. Code and benchmarks are available under the MIT License.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将LTA拆分为三代理协作：Observer从部分视频识别已发生动作，构建双形态记忆——(1)高层的History Action Abstract（人意图与环境状态），(2)低层的History Action Graph（物体状态与时序依赖）；Planner在高、低层历史条件下生成未来动作草案；Verifier依据图结构严谨核验草案与物理可行性并修正不可行动作，形成闭环“Observe-Plan-Verify”。

Result: 在EPIC-Kitchens-55与EGTEA Gaze+基准上，FactCheck在多项指标上稳定超过最新SOTA，显示更强的可行性与准确性。

Conclusion: 以可行性为中心的闭环范式有效闭合“识别-预测-验证”链路，缓解开环方法的物理不一致问题，为具身智能中的长期动作预判提供新路径。

Abstract: Long-term action anticipation (LTA) aims to predict an ordered sequence of future verb-noun actions from a partially observed video. While this task serves as the foundation for embodied intelligence, anticipating physically feasible long-term actions remains a critical challenge. Existing methods, which operate in an open-loop manner, often hallucinate non-existent objects, violate object affordances, or disregard object states, as they lack explicit mechanisms to verify action feasibility against the physical environment. To address this, we propose FactCheck, a novel multi-agent collaboration framework that improves feasibility through a closed-loop "Observe-Plan-Verify" mechanism. FactCheck decomposes the complex LTA task into specialized roles: an Observer that recognizes historical actions from video observations and constructs a dual-form structured memory, comprising a History Action Abstract that captures high-level human intentions and environmental status, and a History Action Graph that encodes object states and temporal dependencies; a Planner that generates draft future actions conditioned on both low-level historical actions and high-level History Action Abstract; and a Verifier that rigorously validates the draft against the History Action Graph and refines infeasible actions. Extensive experiments on the EPIC-Kitchens-55 and EGTEA Gaze+ benchmarks demonstrate that FactCheck consistently outperforms state-of-the-art methods. Our work establishes a new paradigm for feasibility-aware long-term action anticipation, effectively closing the loop of action recognition, action prediction and action verification.

The framework is guided by a variational formulation based on a dehazing decomposition, incorporating a multiplicative residual component to absorb remaining artifacts and a nonlocal gradient-type constraint to preserve structural details and enhance edge sharpness. We provide a theoretical analysis establishing the existence of solution for the associated minimization problem. The proposed unfolding method incorporates Mamba layers to efficiently capture self-similarities in the scene. Experimental results demonstrate that the proposed unfolding approach achieves improved visual quality and competitive quantitative performance compared with recent state-of-the-art methods. ### [38] [Last But Not Least: Boundary Attention CalibratiON for Multimodal KV Cache Compression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14782)
*Tianhao Chen,Yuheng Wu,Kelu Yao,Xiaogang Xu,Xiaobin Hu,Dongman Lee*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出BACON方法，通过结合最后查询注意力与观测窗口注意力并用层内一致性与层间持久性抑制噪声，提升MLLM在激进KV压缩下的性能，平均提升7.5%，最高30.9%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长视觉上下文导致KV缓存膨胀、解码延迟上升。现有基于观测窗口注意力的压缩在激进预算下会把稀疏但关键的视觉证据平均化而被丢弃，需要一种既能找回答案关键证据又能避免噪声误导的机制。

Method: 将“最后查询注意力”(last-query attention)作为补充信号来恢复被观测窗口注意力淡化的关键证据；再通过两种正则/校准策略抑制其无关噪声：层内一致性(intra-layer coherence)与层间持久性(inter-layer persistence)；形成即插即用的BACON，对多种KV压缩方法进行校准以选择更应保留的视觉token。

Result: 在多种基准、模型、预算与压缩方法上，尤其在最激进的压缩预算下，平均性能提升7.5%，最高可达30.9%。

Conclusion: BACON能稳定增强多模态KV压缩时的保真度，在不改变模型结构的前提下有效降低长视觉上下文带来的计算与延迟开销，同时保持或提升问答准确性。

Abstract: Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) achieve strong vision-language reasoning, but long visual contexts enlarge the KV cache and increase decoding latency. Existing compression methods rely on observation window attention for stable token-importance estimation, yet this aggregation can dilute sparse visual evidence and discard answer-critical tokens under aggressive compression. Therefore, we identify last-query attention as a complementary source for recovering such evidence, but its answer-irrelevant signals can mislead retention. We propose BACON, a plug-and-play method that calibrates observation window attention with last-query evidence and suppresses isolated noise via intra-layer coherence and inter-layer persistence. Across diverse benchmarks, models, budgets, and compression methods, BACON improves multimodal KV compression by 7.5% on average under the most aggressive budget, with gains up to 30.9%.

### [39] [The Vision Encoder as a Privacy Boundary: Visual-Token Side Channels in Encoder-Free Vision-Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14783)
*Chenyu Zhou,Qiliang Jiang,Shuning Wu,Xu Zhou*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 作者发现无编码器的视觉-语言模型会将图像补丁直接注入语言模型token流，导致中间视觉token与KV缓存可被逆推还原原图细节，泄露文本等敏感信息；而带视觉编码器的模型难以还原精确字符串。关键泄露因子是视觉token格的空间采样保真度，尤其字符方向采样密度。常见数值级防护（加噪、量化）无效，缓解需降低空间采样或保留编码器作为隐私边界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实务中VLM常用于文档/图片理解，服务端为加速会缓存KV；若中间视觉表示或缓存被访问，是否能重构敏感信息（如验证码/接入码）尚不清楚。作者动机是评估“去编码器”架构的隐私攻击面与泄露路径，并量化导致泄露的架构性因素。

Method: 提出“token访问对手”威胁模型：攻击者获取中间视觉token流或早层KV缓存。对两种无编码器VLM（Gemma4、Fuyu）进行反演，重建图像并识别隐藏访问码；与配对的有编码器VLM作对照。进行消融：控制token/值数量、空间采样密度（尤其字符方向）等；测试鲁棒性（杂乱、文档退化、零样本到公开文档），并评估数值级防御（加性噪声、量化）。

Result: 无编码器模型的视觉token流与Gemma4第0层KV缓存可被直接反演，恢复可读字符串与可辨结构；对照的有编码器模型仅能定位区域无法还原精确字符串。决定性因素是空间采样保真度而非token/值计数；字符方向采样密度越高，泄露越强。攻击在杂乱与退化下仍有效，且对加噪、量化等数值防御具有抗性。

Conclusion: 移除视觉编码器会显著扩大隐私攻击面：中间视觉token与KV缓存构成可被反演的侧信道。有效缓解需牺牲空间采样保真度（降采样/糙化）或保留/引入视觉编码器作为语义瓶颈；单纯数值级扰动不足。部署VLM应将是否去编码器视为一项隐私一等公民决策，并限制KV缓存持久化与访问。

Abstract: A vision encoder compresses image pixels into semantic embeddings, implicitly acting as a privacy boundary by preserving semantic content while attenuating pixel-local detail required for exact text recovery. Encoder-free vision-language models (VLMs) remove this boundary by routing image patches directly into the language-model token stream, thereby exposing an architectural privacy attack surface: intermediate visual tokens become a pre-output side channel. Under a token-access adversary, decoders invert visual-token streams from two encoder-free VLMs, Gemma4 and Fuyu, recovering recognizable image structure and readable held-out access codes, whereas matched encoder-based controls localize target regions but recover no exact strings. Within-model ablations show that the operative factor is spatial sampling fidelity of the visual-token grid, especially character-direction sampling density, rather than token or value count. The leakage is not limited to exported tokens: Gemma4 layer-0 key-value cache tensors are directly invertible, placing the side channel within KV caches commonly persisted by production serving stacks for decoding efficiency. The attack survives clutter, realistic document degradation, and zero-shot transfer to public document images, and it resists value-level defenses such as additive noise and quantization. Effective mitigation must therefore reduce spatial sampling, making removal of the vision encoder a first-class privacy decision in VLM deployment.

</details>


### [40] [Vision-Encoder Behavioral Fingerprints of Image-to-Image Generative Models: A Training-Paradigm-Driven Taxonomy of Six Commercial APIs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14787)
*Hunter Hill*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 研究比较6个图像到图像AI系统在内容自适应、子JND级别对抗扰动下的稳健性，用冻结的DINOv2 ViT-B/14 token距离对输出与干净参考的差异进行量化，发现它们在(patch_mean, ssim_clean)二维空间上分成两类行为带：编辑训练的模型聚成紧致带，采样时适配的T2I基座模型形成“漂移带”。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在实际生产环境中，图像编辑/转化系统会遭遇微弱但可感知阈值以下（sub-JND）的扰动，这些扰动可能系统性地改变输出。需要一个统一、可量化的稳健性评测框架来比较不同体系（专门编辑模型 vs 由文本到图像模型临时适配的img2img）对这类扰动的敏感性与一致性。

Method: 构建内容自适应的子JND对抗扰动管线，对来自COCO、CelebA-HQ以及AI生成图像的3,588个调用样本进行测试；对六个系统（gpt-image-1、Gemini 2.5 Flash Image、Flux Kontext、SDXL img2img、SD3 img2img、Qwen Image Edit）产生的输出，用冻结的DINOv2 ViT-B/14的token距离与干净参考对比评分；在(patch_mean, ssim_clean)二维指标平面上分析其行为分布与聚类。

Result: 六个系统在指标平面上分成两条行为带：编辑训练的模型（Flux Kontext、Qwen Edit、Gemini）聚成紧密、图像不变的“稳定带”；而基于T2I并在采样时适配的模型（SDXL、SD3、gpt-image-1）形成偏移更大的“漂移带”。

Conclusion: 编辑训练的img2img模型在子JND扰动下更一致、更稳健；而由T2I基座临时适配的img2img在相同条件下更易产生输出漂移。该评测框架与发现为选择生产级图像编辑系统与其鲁棒性优化提供了实证依据。

Abstract: We study six production image-to-image AI systems (gpt-image-1, Gemini 2.5 Flash Image, Flux Kontext, SDXL img2img, SD3 img2img, and Qwen Image Edit) under a content-adaptive sub-JND adversarial perturbation pipeline, scoring all outputs by frozen DINOv2 ViT-B/14 token distances against clean references. Across a 3,588-call corpus spanning COCO photographs, CelebA-HQ portraits, and AI-generated inputs, the six systems partition into two image-invariant behavioral bands on a 2D (patch_mean, ssim_clean) plane: edit-trained models (Flux Kontext, Qwen Edit, Gemini) cluster in a tight band, while T2I-base models adapted at sampling time (SDXL, SD3, gpt-image-1) cluster in a drift band.

### [41] [Efficient Reinforcement for Visual-Textual Thinking with Discrete Diffusion Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14792)
*Yoonjeon Kim,Yuhta Takida,Chieh-Hsin Lai,Eunho Yang,Yuki Mitsufuji*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出用多模态离散扩散模型替代自回归统一模型进行RL后训练，以局部视觉编辑实现高效视觉rollout；并用“分解奖励分配”分别给文本与视觉段落打分，避免跨模态干扰，效率更高、效果更好。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有统一多模态AR模型在交错视觉-文本推理中，视觉推理需整图再生成，rollout开销大；且RL中常用的联合奖励会把同一奖励信号同时施加到图像与文本序列，引入无关跨模态干扰，限制性能。

Method: 1) 用多模态离散扩散模型做统一生成，并在RL（如GRPO）中利用局部视觉编辑替代整图再生成，实现更便宜的视觉rollout；2) 训练时将交错序列划分为文本段与视觉段，采用“分解奖励分配”，分别依据各自的奖励信号更新对应参数，避免跨模态梯度干扰。

Result: 相较AR基线，视觉rollout计算在GRPO中减少26.9%，性能仅小幅下降；在奖励设计上，分解奖励分配相较联合奖励提升11.2%，相较未RL的基座模型提升38.04%。

Conclusion: 离散扩散统一模型在RL后训练的交错多模态推理中可通过局部编辑显著降低rollout成本；同时，按模态分解奖励能抑制跨模态干扰并显著提升效果，兼顾效率与性能，优于传统AR与联合奖励方案。

Abstract: RL-based post-training has been widely adopted to enable interleaved visual and textual reasoning in unified multimodal models capable of both text and image generation. However, most existing approaches are built upon autoregressive (AR) unified models, which require full image regeneration during visual reasoning. In this work, we demonstrate that multimodal discrete diffusion models are effective alternatives to AR models for reinforcement learning in interleaved reasoning, owing to their ability to perform efficient visual rollouts via localized visual editing rather than full image-token regeneration. This reduces rollout computation during GRPO by 26.9\% compared to AR baselines, with minimal performance drop. Despite the improved efficiency, we find that joint reward assignment, which employs a shared reward signal across modalities, introduces cross-modal interference between unrelated image and text token sequences during RL updates. To address this issue, we propose factorized reward assignment, a strategy that assigns rewards independently to text and vision segments. With factorized reward assignment, our RL approach achieves an 11.2% improvement over joint reward assignment and a 38.04% improvement over the base model.

### [42] [Position: The Systemic Lack of Agency in Visual Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14795)
*Yizhao Huang,Haoyang Chen,Shiqin Wang,Pohsun Huang,Jiayuan Li,Haoyuan Du,Yandong Shi,Zheng Wang,Zhixiang Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文指出当前视觉-语言模型（VLM）因缺乏“能动性”（主动探索与自导式分析）而在隐式推理上受限，并提出V-IRD基准专门诊断这一短板：要求模型通过自主视觉分析而非被动检索来作答。实验发现主流VLM虽检索强，但难以利用参照物与自发关注隐含证据，显示语义识别≠主动视觉探索。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 人类视觉理解依赖在不完全信息下主动发现并使用隐含线索的能力；而现有VLM多被训练与评测为“被动语义检索”，导致隐式推理（需自发寻找证据、跨帧/区域联结）的关键能力未被衡量或培养。

Method: 提出Visual Implicit Reasoning Diagnosing Benchmark (V-IRD)：设计任务强制模型在无显式目标指引下，通过自主视觉分析、参照物定位与证据采样完成推理；以现有主流VLM进行评测，对比其被动检索能力与主动探索需求下的表现差异。

Result: 在V-IRD上，多数强势VLM表现显著下滑：难以使用参照物、难以将注意力转向需自导式探查的视觉证据；显示其隐式推理与主动探索能力不足，即便在语义识别与检索上成绩优异。

Conclusion: 当前VLM存在“强检索、弱能动”的结构性缺陷；隐式推理需要能动性的主动视觉探索。V-IRD填补评测空白并揭示关键差距，提示未来需在训练与架构上引入具备能动性与自导式感知-推理循环的设计。

Abstract: This paper argues that a systemic lack of Agency constrains the implicit reasoning capabilities of current Vision-Language Models (VLMs). Implicit reasoning refers to the ability to autonomously discover and utilize hidden visual evidence to bridge information gaps, rather than merely relying on explicitly specified targets. This capacity underlies human visual understanding and everyday reasoning. We argue that this limitation arises from a tendency to approach visual reasoning primarily as passive semantic retrieval, rather than as active, situated reasoning that depends on autonomous visual exploration. As a result, most existing benchmarks primarily assess Passive Capacity, leaving this aspect of reasoning largely unmeasured. To address this gap, we introduce the Visual Implicit Reasoning Diagnosing Benchmark (V-IRD), which targets this missing quadrant by requiring models to derive answers strictly through autonomous visual analysis. Our results show that, despite strong retrieval abilities, prominent VLMs struggle to utilize reference objects and to attend to visual evidence that requires self-directed inquiry. Simply put, strong semantic recognition does not equate to active visual exploration, revealing a critical gap in current VLMs. More information can be found at https://haoychen.github.io/Implicit-Reasoning/
