### [252] [Qwen-RobotWorld Technical Report: Unifying Embodied World Modeling through Language-Conditioned Video Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17030)
*Jie Zhang,Xiaoyue Chen,Anzhe Chen,Chenxu Lv,Deqing Li,Gengze Zhou,Hang Yin,Haoqi Yuan,Haoyang Li,Jiahao Li,Jiazhao Zhang,Jingren Zhou,Kaiyuan Gao,Kun Yan,Lihan Jiang,Ningyuan Tang,Pei Lin,Qihang Peng,Shengming Yin,Tianhe Wu,Tianyi Yan,Xiao Xu,Yan Shu,Yanran Zhang,Ye Wang,Yi Wang,Yilei Chen,Yixian Xu,Yiyang Huang,Yuxiang Chen,Zekai Zhang,Zhendong Wang,Zhixing Lei,Zhixuan Liang,Zihao Liu,Zikai Zhou,Xiong-Hui Chen,Chenfei Wu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: Qwen-RobotWorld 提出一个以自然语言为统一动作接口的语言条件视频世界模型，能在多种具身场景中从当前观测预测物理一致的未来视觉轨迹，并在数据合成、评测环境与语言引导规划上展现强应用潜力，在多项基准上取得领先表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有世界模型与具身智能往往分散在特定任务/形态，缺乏统一的语言接口与跨领域泛化能力；同时，训练与评测缺少大规模、跨具身的动作-语言标注数据与通用框架，以支持合成数据增强、可扩展评测及语言驱动的下游控制。

Method: 三部分设计：a) Double-Stream MMDiT + MLLM 动作编码：60层双流扩散Transformer，通过逐层联合注意力将冻结的 Qwen2.5-VL 语义与视频VAE潜变量耦合，实现语言到视觉未来的条件预测；b) Embodied World Knowledge（EWK）语料：包含约8.6M视频-文本（200M+帧），覆盖20+具身类型、500+动作类别，并提供动作-语言映射；c) General+Expert 递进式课程学习：先学通用视觉先验，再在共享语言接口下注入具身专业化。

Result: 在 EWMBench 与 DreamGen Bench 总体排名第1；在 WorldModelBench 与 PBench 上超过所有开源模型；在 RoboTwin-IF 的零样本评测中展示稳健的泛化与多视角一致性。

Conclusion: 语言作为统一动作接口的世界模型可在多具身领域实现物理一致的未来视觉预测，支持合成数据、可扩展评测与语言引导规划；所提模型与数据/训练策略在多基准上验证了其通用性与领先性能。

Abstract: We introduce Qwen-RobotWorld, a language-conditioned video world model for embodied intelligence. With natural language as a unified action interface, it predicts physically grounded future visual trajectories from current observations across robotic manipulation, autonomous driving, indoor navigation, and human-to-robot transfer. This unified formulation provides three promising application directions: synthetic data generation for policy training augmentation, scalable virtual environments for policy evaluation, and language-guided planning signals for downstream robot control. This is achieved through a three-part design: a) Double-Stream MMDiT with MLLM Action Encoding, where a 60-layer double-stream diffusion transformer couples frozen Qwen2.5-VL semantics with video-VAE latents through layer-wise joint attention; b) Embodied World Knowledge (EWK), an 8.6M video-text corpus (200M+ frames) with action-language mapping over 20+ embodiments and 500+ action categories; and c) General+Expert Progressive Curriculum, a two-stage training strategy that first learns general visual priors and then injects embodied specialization under a shared language interface. Extensive results show strong competitiveness: ranks 1st overall on EWMBench and DreamGen Bench, outperforms all open-source models on WorldModelBench and PBench. Additional zero-shot analyses on RoboTwin-IF benchmark further support robust generalization and multi-view consistency.

</details>


### [253] [The Importance of Phase in Neural Representations: An Internal Oppenheim-Lim Test of Image Classifiers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17037)
*Alper Yıldırım*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文通过在神经网络层内“相位/符号-幅度移植”实验，因果检验图像身份信息主要由相位/符号承载而非幅度；多数架构（PRISM2D, GFNet, ViT-B/16）预测随相位/符号供体变化，ResNet-50在ReLU后看似例外，但在ReLU前干预揭示后期块存在强符号编码；读出更偏向通道均值（DC）信息。结果给出CNN与注意力模型“纹理-形状”差异的机制性解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典结果表明自然图像的傅里叶相位决定可识别性，而幅度信息对身份作用小。作者想问：现代深度视觉模型在其隐藏层是否也复现这种“相位>幅度”的不对称性？并希望用因果方式验证（而非相关性）并解释不同架构（卷积 vs 注意力）的纹理-形状偏好差异。

Method: 提出分层干预：在指定网络层，取两张图像A、B，将A的相位（或激活符号）与B的幅度（或激活大小）组合成合成激活，前向传播并观察预测更像哪张图。对PRISM2D、GFNet、ViT-B/16与ResNet-50分别实施。为ResNet，比较ReLU前后干预，检测潜在符号编码；加入DC-only（仅通道空间平均）与“删除图像特异幅度”的对照，排除幅度退化或无关的平凡解释。

Result: - 在PRISM2D、GFNet、ViT-B/16：预测稳定跟随相位/符号供体；移除图像特异幅度几乎不降准，说明身份主要由相位/符号承载，幅度对读出基本可舍。- ResNet-50：ReLU后移植符号无效，似乎违背模式；但在ReLU前干预显现后期残差块存在强符号编码；DC-only对照表明读出主要依赖通道级空间平均（全局池化）信息。- 额外对照确认幅度仍与图像有关，排除“幅度无信息”的平凡情形。

Conclusion: 不同架构共享“相位/符号即身份”的编码，但因非线性整流与读出几何（如全局平均池化 vs 注意力读出）使该代码在不同基底上显现，提供了CNN与注意力模型在纹理-形状偏好差异的机制性解释。

Abstract: Oppenheim and Lim (1981) showed that natural images stay recognizable when reconstructed from their Fourier phase alone, while the magnitude carries little of their identity. We ask whether trained image classifiers reproduce this asymmetry inside their hidden layers, and we test it causally: given two images, we transplant the phase of one onto the magnitude of the other at a chosen layer and record which image the prediction follows. In PRISM2D, GFNet, and ViT-B/16 the prediction follows the phase or sign donor, and deleting all image-specific magnitude barely moves accuracy, so identity rides on phase while image-specific magnitude is largely dispensable to the readout. ResNet-50 at first seems to break the pattern, because transplanting sign after its ReLUs does nothing; a fair intervention before the ReLU reveals a strong latent sign code in the late blocks, and a DC-only control shows the readout consumes a channel-wise spatial average. Controls rule out the trivial case in which magnitude simply stops depending on the image. The architectures therefore share a phase/sign identity code but expose it in different bases, set by rectification and readout geometry, which gives a mechanistic account of the texture--shape gap between CNNs and attention models.

</details>


### [254] [BRDFusion: Physics Meets Generation for Urban Scene Inverse Rendering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17049)
*Yi-Ruei Liu,Jie-Ying Lee,Zheng-Hui Huang,Yu-Lun Liu,Chih-Hao Lin*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出BRDFusion，将物理可控的逆/正向渲染与生成式先验结合，既重建一致的场景属性又在渲染阶段去噪修复伪影，实现高质量、可控的视频合成与编辑，并优于基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有两类方法各有缺陷：物理基的逆渲染可控但易出现重建与渲染伪影；生成式视频模型逼真度高但一致性与可控性差。需要统一框架兼顾物理一致性、可控性与感知质量。

Method: 构建双分支统一框架：1) 逆渲染阶段以物理模型恢复显式且一致的场景属性（几何、BRDF、光照），并引入生成式先验缓解优化歧义；2) 正向渲染阶段用物理模型从场景配置产生可控渲染，再用生成模型进行去噪与伪影修复，从而融合物理可控性与生成逼真度。

Result: 在真实与合成城市视频上，生成的视频质量与一致性优于基线；同时支持精确控制与编辑操作（新视角重光照、夜景模拟、动态目标插入与编辑）。

Conclusion: 物理建模+生成先验的统一框架能在保持可控与一致的同时显著提升视频质量，适合多种城市场景编辑与仿真任务。

Abstract: Inverse rendering of urban scenes from captured videos enables numerous applications, including content creation and autonomous driving simulation. Physically-based rendering methods follow and control lighting physics, but suffer from reconstruction and rendering artifacts. While generative models produce realistic videos, they offer limited consistency and controllability. We present BRDFusion, a unified framework that combines two complementary models for inverse and forward rendering. Specifically, BRDFusion recovers explicit, consistent scene properties with physical modeling and alleviates optimization ambiguity with generative priors. During forward rendering, the physical model provides controllable rendering from the scene configuration, and the generative model denoises and fixes artifacts. Therefore, our method produces high-quality videos while allowing precise control, outperforming baselines in real and synthetic scenes. Moreover, BRDFusion supports novel-view relighting, night simulation, and dynamic object insertion/editing. Project page: https://shigon255.github.io/brdfusion-page/

</details>
